Candara Regular (Candara.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Candara', Everything looks good.

Candara Regular (Candara.ttf)

name

Mac NID 8/13

License text

Cannot check license text because of unkown entity 'Microsoft Corporation' (NID8). Please verify against job spec.
Mac NID 13 is:
Microsoft supplied font. You may use this font to create, display, and print content as permitted by the license terms or terms of use, of the Microsoft product, service, or content in which this font was included. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. Any other use is prohibited.
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Candara Italic (Candarai.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Candara-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Candara Italic (Candarai.ttf)

name

MS NID 7

Test Trademark

Current trademark entry is:
'Candara is either a registered trademark or a trademark of Microsoft Corporation in the United States and/or other countries.'
Trademark does not follow Monotype standards.
Please verify agains spec.
More infos here:
Monotype Manufacturing Settings (google doc)

Error

Candara Italic (Candarai.ttf)

name

MS NID 8

Manufactur (NID 8) should be Monotype IP

MS NID 8 is 'Microsoft Corporation', but should be one of these: 'Monotype Imaging Inc.', 'Monotype Imaging Inc', 'Monotype ITC Inc.', 'Monotype Hong Kong Limited', 'Monotype Limited', 'Monotype KK', 'Monotype Solutions India Private Limited', 'Monotype GmbH', 'MyFonts Inc.', 'MyFonts Inc', 'Fontsmith Ltd.', 'Fontsmith Ltd'.

Warning

Candara Italic (Candarai.ttf)

name

MS NID 10, Description

'Description' has leading or trailing spaces.

leading or trailing spaces are highlighted with [  ]:
'Candara is a casual humanist sans with verticals showing a graceful entasis on stems, high-branching arcades in the lowercase, large apertures in all open forms, and unique ogee curves on diagonals. The resultant texture is lively but not intrusive, and makes for a[  ]friendly and readable text.'

Error

Candara Italic (Candarai.ttf)

name

MS NID 8/13

License text

Cannot check license text because of unkown entity 'Microsoft Corporation' (NID8). Please verify against job spec.
MS NID 13 is:
Microsoft supplied font. You may use this font to create, display, and print content as permitted by the license terms or terms of use, of the Microsoft product, service, or content in which this font was included. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. Any other use is prohibited.
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Error

Any other use is prohibited.
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Candara Bold Italic (Candaraz.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Candara-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Mac NID 8/13

License text

Cannot check license text because of unkown entity 'Microsoft Corporation' (NID8). Please verify against job spec.
Mac NID 13 is:
Microsoft supplied font. You may use this font to create, display, and print content as permitted by the license terms or terms of use, of the Microsoft product, service, or content in which this font was included. You may only (i) embed this font in content as permitted by the embedding restrictions included in this font; and (ii) temporarily download this font to a printer or other output device to help print content. Any other use is prohibited.
, most common Monotype license test is:
This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. You have obtained this font software either directly from Monotype or together with software distributed by one of the licensees of Monotype. This software is a valuable asset of Monotype. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

kern

Warning

Candara Regular (Candara.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.
